<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="token-estimation">Token Estimation<a href="#token-estimation" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Token Estimation" title="Direct link to Token Estimation" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>By default, the HTTP provider does not provide token usage statistics since it&#x27;s designed for general HTTP APIs that may not return token information. However, you can enable optional token estimation to get approximate token counts for cost tracking and analysis. Token estimation is automatically enabled when running redteam scans so you can track approximate costs without additional configuration.</p>
<p>Token estimation uses a simple word-based counting method with configurable multipliers. This provides a rough approximation that&#x27;s useful for basic cost estimation and usage tracking.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_WCGJ alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>Accuracy</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>Word-based estimation provides approximate token counts. For precise token counting, implement custom logic in your <code>transformResponse</code> function using a proper tokenizer library.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="when-to-use-token-estimation">When to Use Token Estimation<a href="#when-to-use-token-estimation" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to When to Use Token Estimation" title="Direct link to When to Use Token Estimation" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>Token estimation is useful when:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Your API doesn&#x27;t return token usage information</li>
<li class="">You need basic cost estimates for budget tracking</li>
<li class="">You want to monitor usage patterns across different prompts</li>
<li class="">You&#x27;re migrating from an API that provides token counts</li>
</ul>
<p>Don&#x27;t use token estimation when:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Your API already provides accurate token counts (use <code>transformResponse</code> instead)</li>
<li class="">You need precise token counts for billing</li>
<li class="">You&#x27;re working with non-English text where word counting is less accurate</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="basic-token-estimation">Basic Token Estimation<a href="#basic-token-estimation" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Basic Token Estimation" title="Direct link to Basic Token Estimation" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>Enable basic token estimation with default settings:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://example.com/api&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">body</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">prompt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{prompt}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tokenEstimation</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">enabled</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token boolean important" style="color:#36acaa">true</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>This will use word-based estimation with a multiplier of 1.3 for both prompt and completion tokens.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="custom-multipliers">Custom Multipliers<a href="#custom-multipliers" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Custom Multipliers" title="Direct link to Custom Multipliers" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>Configure a custom multiplier for more accurate estimation based on your specific use case:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://example.com/api&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">body</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">prompt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{prompt}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tokenEstimation</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">enabled</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token boolean important" style="color:#36acaa">true</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">multiplier</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">1.5</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Adjust based on your content complexity</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><strong>Multiplier Guidelines:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="">Start with default <code>1.3</code> and adjust based on actual usage</li>
<li class="">Technical/code content may need higher multipliers (1.5-2.0)</li>
<li class="">Simple conversational text may work with lower multipliers (1.1-1.3)</li>
<li class="">Monitor actual vs. estimated usage to calibrate</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="integration-with-transform-response">Integration with Transform Response<a href="#integration-with-transform-response" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Integration with Transform Response" title="Direct link to Integration with Transform Response" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>Token estimation works alongside response transforms. If your <code>transformResponse</code> returns token usage information, the estimation will be skipped:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://example.com/api&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tokenEstimation</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">enabled</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token boolean important" style="color:#36acaa">true</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Will be ignored if transformResponse provides tokenUsage</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">transformResponse</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">|</span><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">        {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          output: json.choices[0].message.content,</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          tokenUsage: {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            prompt: json.usage.prompt_tokens,</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            completion: json.usage.completion_tokens,</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            total: json.usage.total_tokens</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          }</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">        }</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="custom-token-counting">Custom Token Counting<a href="#custom-token-counting" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Custom Token Counting" title="Direct link to Custom Token Counting" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>For accurate token counting, implement it in your <code>transformResponse</code> function:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://example.com/api&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">transformResponse</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">|</span><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">        (json, text, context) =&gt; {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          // Use a proper tokenizer library for accuracy</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          const promptTokens = customTokenizer.encode(context.vars.prompt).length;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          const completionTokens = customTokenizer.encode(json.response).length;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          </span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          return {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            output: json.response,</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            tokenUsage: {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">              prompt: promptTokens,</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">              completion: completionTokens,</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">              total: promptTokens + completionTokens,</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">              numRequests: 1</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            }</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          };</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">        }</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>You can also load custom logic from a file:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://example.com/api&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">transformResponse</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;file://token-counter.js&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Example <code>token-counter.js</code>:</p>
<div class="language-javascript codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token parameter">json</span><span class="token parameter punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token parameter"> text</span><span class="token parameter punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token parameter"> context</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=&gt;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#00009f">const</span><span class="token plain"> responseText </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain"> json</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token plain">response </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">||</span><span class="token plain"> text</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token literal-property property" style="color:#36acaa">output</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> responseText</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token literal-property property" style="color:#36acaa">tokenUsage</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token literal-property property" style="color:#d73a49">encode</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token plain">responseText</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token plain">length</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token literal-property property" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token plain">length </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">+</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">encode</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token plain">responseText</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token plain">length</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token literal-property property" style="color:#36acaa">numRequests</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">1</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="configuration-options">Configuration Options<a href="#configuration-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Configuration Options" title="Direct link to Configuration Options" translate="no"></a></h3>
<table><thead><tr><th>Option</th><th>Type</th><th>Default</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>enabled</td><td>boolean</td><td>false (true in redteam mode)</td><td>Enable or disable token estimation</td></tr><tr><td>multiplier</td><td>number</td><td>1.3</td><td>Multiplier applied to word count (adjust for complexity)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="example-cost-tracking">Example: Cost Tracking<a href="#example-cost-tracking" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Example: Cost Tracking" title="Direct link to Example: Cost Tracking" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>Here&#x27;s a complete example for cost tracking with token estimation:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://api.example.com/v1/generate&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">method</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> POST</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">headers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">Authorization</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;Bearer {{env.API_KEY}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">Content-Type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;application/json&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">body</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">model</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;custom-model&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">prompt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{prompt}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">max_tokens</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">100</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tokenEstimation</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">enabled</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token boolean important" style="color:#36acaa">true</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">multiplier</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">1.4</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Adjusted based on testing</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">transformResponse</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">|</span><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">        {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          output: json.generated_text,</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          cost: (json.usage?.total_tokens || 0) * 0.0001 // $0.0001 per token</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">        }</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="tlshttps-configuration">TLS/HTTPS Configuration<a href="#tlshttps-configuration" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to TLS/HTTPS Configuration" title="Direct link to TLS/HTTPS Configuration" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>The HTTP provider supports custom TLS certificate configuration for secure HTTPS connections. This enables:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Custom CA certificates for verifying server certificates</li>
<li class="">Client certificates for mutual TLS authentication</li>
<li class="">PFX/PKCS12 certificate bundles</li>
<li class="">Fine-grained control over TLS security settings</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="basic-tls-configuration">Basic TLS Configuration<a href="#basic-tls-configuration" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Basic TLS Configuration" title="Direct link to Basic TLS Configuration" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>Configure custom CA certificates to verify server certificates:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://api.example.com/secure&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tls</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;/path/to/ca-cert.pem&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Custom CA certificate</span><span style="color:#36acaa">true</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Verify server certificate (default: true)</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="mutual-tls-mtls">Mutual TLS (mTLS)<a href="#mutual-tls-mtls" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Mutual TLS (mTLS)" title="Direct link to Mutual TLS (mTLS)" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>For APIs requiring client certificate authentication:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">certPath</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;/path/to/client-cert.pem&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;/path/to/ca-cert.pem&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="using-pfxpkcs12-certificates">Using PFX/PKCS12 Certificates<a href="#using-pfxpkcs12-certificates" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Using PFX/PKCS12 Certificates" title="Direct link to Using PFX/PKCS12 Certificates" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>For PFX or PKCS12 certificate bundles, you can either provide a file path or inline base64-encoded content:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tls</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Option 1: Using a file path</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">pfxPath</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;/path/to/certificate.pfx&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token <div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="using-jks-java-keystore-certificates">Using JKS (Java KeyStore) Certificates<a href="#using-jks-java-keystore-certificates" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Using JKS (Java KeyStore) Certificates" title="Direct link to Using JKS (Java KeyStore) Certificates" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>For Java applications using JKS certificates, the provider can automatically extract the certificate and key for TLS:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://secure-api.example.com/v1&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tls</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Option 1: Using a file path</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">jksPath</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;/path/to/keystore.jks&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">passphrase</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{env.JKS_PASSWORD}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Required for JKS</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">keyAlias</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;mykey&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional: specific alias to use</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://secure-api.example.com/v1&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tls</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Option 2: Using inline base64-encoded JKS content</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">jksContent</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;MIIJKQIBAzCCCO8GCSqGSIb3DQEHA...&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Base64-encoded JKS content</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">passphrase</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{env.JKS_PASSWORD}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">keyAlias</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;client-cert&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional: defaults to first available key</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The JKS file is processed using the <code>jks-js</code> library, which automatically:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Extracts the certificate and private key from the keystore</li>
<li class="">Converts them to PEM format for use with TLS</li>
<li class="">Selects the appropriate key based on the alias (or uses the first available)</li>
</ul>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_WCGJ alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>info</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>JKS support requires the <code>jks-js</code> package. Install it with:</p><div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">npm</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">install</span><span class="token plain"> jks-js</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="advanced-tls-options">Advanced TLS Options<a href="#advanced-tls-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Advanced TLS Options" title="Direct link to Advanced TLS Options" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>Fine-tune TLS connection parameters:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">certPath</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">rejectUnauthorized</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="inline-certificates">Inline Certificates<a href="#inline-certificates" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Inline Certificates" title="Direct link to Inline Certificates" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>You can provide certificates directly in the configuration instead of file paths:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" <h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="multiple-ca-certificates">Multiple CA Certificates<a href="#multiple-ca-certificates" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Multiple CA Certificates" title="Direct link to Multiple CA Certificates" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>Support for multiple CA certificates in the trust chain:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">|</span><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            -----BEGIN CERTIFICATE-----</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            [Intermediate CA certificate content]</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            -----END CERTIFICATE-----</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="self-signed-certificates">Self-Signed Certificates<a href="#self-signed-certificates" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Self-Signed Certificates" title="Direct link to Self-Signed Certificates" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>For development/testing with self-signed certificates:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://localhost:8443/api&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tls</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">rejectUnauthorized</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token boolean important" style="color:#36acaa">false</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Accept self-signed certificates (NOT for production!)</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-warning admonition_WCGJ alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>warning</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><p>Setting <code>rejectUnauthorized: false</code> disables certificate verification and should <strong>never</strong> be used in production environments as it makes connections vulnerable to man-in-the-middle attacks.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="environment-variables">Environment Variables<a href="#environment-variables" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Environment Variables" title="Direct link to Environment Variables" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>Use environment variables for sensitive certificate data:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://api.example.com/v1&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">tls</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">certPath</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{env.CLIENT_CERT_PATH}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">keyPath</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{env.CLIENT_KEY_PATH}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">passphrase</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{env.CERT_PASSPHRASE}}&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="tls-configuration-options">TLS Configuration Options<a href="#tls-configuration-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to TLS Configuration Options" title="Direct link to TLS Configuration Options" translate="no"></a></h3>
<table><thead><tr><th>Option</th><th>Type</th><th>Default</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>ca</td><td>string | string[]</td><td>-</td><td>CA certificate(s) for verifying server certificates</td></tr><tr><td>caPath</td><td>string</td><td>-</td><td>Path to CA certificate file</td></tr><tr><td>cert</td><td>string | string[]</td><td>-</td><td>Client certificate(s) for mutual TLS</td></tr><tr><td>certPath</td><td>string</td><td>-</td><td>Path to client certificate file</td></tr><tr><td>key</td><td>string | string[]</td><td>-</td><td>Private key(s) for client certificate</td></tr><tr><td>keyPath</td><td>string</td><td>-</td><td>Path to private key file</td></tr><tr><td>pfx</td><td>string | Buffer</td><td>-</td><td>PFX/PKCS12 certificate bundle (base64-encoded string or Buffer for inline content)</td></tr><tr><td>pfxPath</td><td>string</td><td>-</td><td>Path to PFX/PKCS12 file</td></tr><tr><td>jksPath</td><td>string</td><td>-</td><td>Path to JKS keystore file</td></tr><tr><td>jksContent</td><td>string</td><td>-</td><td>Base64-encoded JKS keystore content</td></tr><tr><td>keyAlias</td><td>string</td><td>-</td><td>Alias of the key to use from JKS (defaults to first available)</td></tr><tr><td>passphrase</td><td>string</td><td>-</td><td>Passphrase for encrypted private key, PFX, or JKS</td></tr><tr><td>rejectUnauthorized</td><td>boolean</td><td>true</td><td>If true, verify server certificate against CA</td></tr><tr><td>servername</td><td>string</td><td>-</td><td>Server name for SNI (Server Name Indication) TLS extension</td></tr><tr><td>ciphers</td><td>string</td><td>-</td><td>Cipher suite specification (OpenSSL format)</td></tr><tr><td>secureProtocol</td><td>string</td><td>-</td><td>SSL method to use (e.g., &#x27;TLSv1_2_method&#x27;, &#x27;TLSv1_3_method&#x27;)</td></tr><tr><td>minVersion</td><td>string</td><td>-</td><td>Minimum TLS version to allow (e.g., &#x27;TLSv1.2&#x27;, &#x27;TLSv1.3&#x27;)</td></tr><tr><td>maxVersion</td><td>string</td><td>-</td><td>Maximum TLS version to allow (e.g., &#x27;TLSv1.2&#x27;, &#x27;TLSv1.3&#x27;)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_WCGJ alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>info</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><ul>
<li class="">When using client certificates, you must provide both certificate and key (unless using PFX or JKS)</li>
<li class="">PFX and JKS bundles contain both certificate and key, so only the bundle and passphrase are needed</li>
<li class="">The TLS configuration is applied to all HTTPS requests made by this provider</li>
</ul></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="authentication">Authentication<a href="#authentication" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Authentication" title="Direct link to Authentication" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>The HTTP provider supports multiple authentication methods. For specialized cases, use custom hooks or custom providers.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="bearer-token">Bearer Token<a href="#bearer-token" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Bearer Token" title="Direct link to Bearer Token" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>For APIs that accept a static bearer token:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://api.example.com/v1/chat&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">body</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">prompt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{prompt}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">auth</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> bearer</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">token</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{env.API_TOKEN}}&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The provider adds an <code>Authorization: Bearer &lt;token&gt;</code> header to each request.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="api-key">API Key<a href="#api-key" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to API Key" title="Direct link to API Key" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>For APIs that use API key authentication, you can place the key in either a header or query parameter:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://api.example.com/v1/chat&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">body</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">prompt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{prompt}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">auth</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> api_key</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">keyName</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;X-API-Key&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">value</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{env.API_KEY}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">placement</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> header </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># or &#x27;query&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>When <code>placement</code> is <code>header</code>, the key is added as a request header. When <code>placement</code> is <code>query</code>, it&#x27;s appended as a URL query parameter.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="basic-authentication">Basic Authentication<a href="#basic-authentication" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Basic Authentication" title="Direct link to Basic Authentication" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>For APIs that use HTTP Basic authentication:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://api.example.com/v1/chat&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">body</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">prompt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{prompt}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">auth</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> basic</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">username</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{env.API_USERNAME}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">password</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{env.API_PASSWORD}}&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The provider Base64-encodes credentials and adds an <code>Authorization: Basic &lt;credentials&gt;</code> header.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="oauth-20">OAuth 2.0<a href="#oauth-20" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to OAuth 2.0" title="Direct link to OAuth 2.0" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>OAuth 2.0 authentication supports <strong>Client Credentials</strong> and <strong>Password</strong> (Resource Owner Password Credentials) grant types.</p>
<p>When a request is made, the provider:</p>
<ol>
<li class="">Checks if a valid access token exists in cache</li>
<li class="">If no token exists or is expired, requests a new one from <code>tokenUrl</code></li>
<li class="">Caches the access token</li>
<li class="">Adds the token to API requests as an <code>Authorization: Bearer &lt;token&gt;</code> header</li>
</ol>
<p>Tokens are refreshed proactively with a 60-second buffer before expiry.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="client-credentials-grant">Client Credentials Grant<a href="#client-credentials-grant" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Client Credentials Grant" title="Direct link to Client Credentials Grant" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>Use this grant type for server-to-server authentication:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">body</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">prompt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> write</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="password-grant">Password Grant<a href="#password-grant" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Password Grant" title="Direct link to Password Grant" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>Use this grant type when authenticating with user credentials:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" atrule" style="color:#00a4db">prompt</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{prompt}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> read</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="token-endpoint-requirements">Token Endpoint Requirements<a href="#token-endpoint-requirements" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Token Endpoint Requirements" title="Direct link to Token Endpoint Requirements" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p>The token endpoint must return a JSON response with an <code>access_token</code> field. If <code>expires_in</code> (lifetime in seconds) is included, the provider uses it to schedule refresh. Otherwise, a 1-hour default is used.</p>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="digital-signature-authentication">Digital Signature Authentication<a href="#digital-signature-authentication" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Digital Signature Authentication" title="Direct link to Digital Signature Authentication" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>For APIs requiring cryptographic request signing, the HTTP provider supports digital signatures with PEM, JKS (Java KeyStore), and PFX certificate formats. The private key is <strong>never sent to Promptfoo</strong> and remains stored locally.</p>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="basic-usage-pem">Basic Usage (PEM)<a href="#basic-usage-pem" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Basic Usage (PEM)" title="Direct link to Basic Usage (PEM)" translate="no"></a></h4>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{signature}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span
