class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">signatureAuth</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> pem</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">privateKeyPath</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;/path/to/private.key&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>When signature authentication is enabled, these template variables become available for use in headers or body:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>{{signature}}</code>: The generated signature (base64-encoded)</li>
<li class=""><code>{{signatureTimestamp}}</code>: Unix timestamp when the signature was generated</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="certificate-formats">Certificate Formats<a href="#certificate-formats" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Certificate Formats" title="Direct link to Certificate Formats" translate="no"></a></h4>
<p><strong>PEM Certificates:</strong></p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">signatureAuth</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">type</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> pem</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">privateKeyPath</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;/path/to/private.key&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Path to PEM file</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># OR inline key:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># privateKey: &#x27;-----BEGIN PRIVATE KEY-----\n...&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><strong>JKS (Java KeyStore):</strong></p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">signatureAuth</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" var</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;your-key-alias&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional: uses first available if not specified</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p><strong>PFX (PKCS#12):</strong></p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">signatureValidityMs</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">300000</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># 5 minutes (default)</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">signatureAlgorithm</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;SHA256&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Default</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">signatureDataTemplate</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{signatureTimestamp}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Default; customize as needed</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">signatureRefreshBufferMs</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">30000</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Optional custom refresh buffer</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_WCGJ alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_GCBg"><span class="admonitionIcon_L39b"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Dependencies</div><div class="admonitionContent_pbrs"><ul>
<li class=""><strong>JKS support</strong> requires the <code>jks-js</code> package: <code>npm install jks-js</code></li>
<li class=""><strong>PFX support</strong> requires the <code>pem</code> package: <code>npm install pem</code></li>
</ul></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="authentication-options-reference">Authentication Options Reference<a href="#authentication-options-reference" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Authentication Options Reference" title="Direct link to Authentication Options Reference" translate="no"></a></h3>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="bearer-token-options">Bearer Token Options<a href="#bearer-token-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Bearer Token Options" title="Direct link to Bearer Token Options" translate="no"></a></h4>
<table><thead><tr><th>Option</th><th>Type</th><th>Required</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>type</td><td>string</td><td>Yes</td><td>Must be <code>&#x27;bearer&#x27;</code></td></tr><tr><td>token</td><td>string</td><td>Yes</td><td>The bearer token</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="api-key-options">API Key Options<a href="#api-key-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to API Key Options" title="Direct link to API Key Options" translate="no"></a></h4>
<table><thead><tr><th>Option</th><th>Type</th><th>Required</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>type</td><td>string</td><td>Yes</td><td>Must be <code>&#x27;api_key&#x27;</code></td></tr><tr><td>keyName</td><td>string</td><td>Yes</td><td>Name of the header or query parameter</td></tr><tr><td>value</td><td>string</td><td>Yes</td><td>The API key value</td></tr><tr><td>placement</td><td>string</td><td>Yes</td><td>Where to place the key: <code>&#x27;header&#x27;</code> or <code>&#x27;query&#x27;</code></td></tr></tbody></table>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="basic-auth-options">Basic Auth Options<a href="#basic-auth-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Basic Auth Options" title="Direct link to Basic Auth Options" translate="no"></a></h4>
<table><thead><tr><th>Option</th><th>Type</th><th>Required</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>type</td><td>string</td><td>Yes</td><td>Must be <code>&#x27;basic&#x27;</code></td></tr><tr><td>username</td><td>string</td><td>Yes</td><td>Username</td></tr><tr><td>password</td><td>string</td><td>Yes</td><td>Password</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="oauth-20-options">OAuth 2.0 Options<a href="#oauth-20-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to OAuth 2.0 Options" title="Direct link to OAuth 2.0 Options" translate="no"></a></h4>
<table><thead><tr><th>Option</th><th>Type</th><th>Required</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>type</td><td>string</td><td>Yes</td><td>Must be <code>&#x27;oauth&#x27;</code></td></tr><tr><td>grantType</td><td>string</td><td>Yes</td><td><code>&#x27;client_credentials&#x27;</code> or <code>&#x27;password&#x27;</code></td></tr><tr><td>tokenUrl</td><td>string</td><td>Yes</td><td>OAuth token endpoint URL</td></tr><tr><td>clientId</td><td>string</td><td>Yes (client_credentials), No (password)</td><td>OAuth client ID</td></tr><tr><td>clientSecret</td><td>string</td><td>Yes (client_credentials), No (password)</td><td>OAuth client secret</td></tr><tr><td>username</td><td>string</td><td>Yes (password grant)</td><td>Username for password grant</td></tr><tr><td>password</td><td>string</td><td>Yes (password grant)</td><td>Password for password grant</td></tr><tr><td>scopes</td><td>string[]</td><td>No</td><td>OAuth scopes to request</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="digital-signature-options">Digital Signature Options<a href="#digital-signature-options" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Digital Signature Options" title="Direct link to Digital Signature Options" translate="no"></a></h4>
<table><thead><tr><th>Option</th><th>Type</th><th>Required</th><th>Default</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>type</td><td>string</td><td>No</td><td><code>&#x27;pem&#x27;</code></td><td>Certificate type: <code>&#x27;pem&#x27;</code>, <code>&#x27;jks&#x27;</code>, or <code>&#x27;pfx&#x27;</code></td></tr><tr><td>privateKeyPath</td><td>string</td><td>No*</td><td>-</td><td>Path to PEM private key file (PEM only)</td></tr><tr><td>privateKey</td><td>string</td><td>No*</td><td>-</td><td>Inline PEM private key string (PEM only)</td></tr><tr><td>keystorePath</td><td>string</td><td>No*</td><td>-</td><td>Path to JKS keystore file (JKS only)</td></tr><tr><td>keystoreContent</td><td>string</td><td>No*</td><td>-</td><td>Base64-encoded JKS keystore content (JKS only)</td></tr><tr><td>keystorePassword</td><td>string</td><td>No</td><td>-</td><td>JKS password (or use <code>PROMPTFOO_JKS_PASSWORD</code> env var)</td></tr><tr><td>keyAlias</td><td>string</td><td>No</td><td>First available</td><td>JKS key alias (JKS only)</td></tr><tr><td>pfxPath</td><td>string</td><td>No*</td><td>-</td><td>Path to PFX certificate file (PFX only)</td></tr><tr><td>pfxPassword</td><td>string</td><td>No</td><td>-</td><td>PFX password (or use <code>PROMPTFOO_PFX_PASSWORD</code> env var)</td></tr><tr><td>certPath</td><td>string</td><td>No*</td><td>-</td><td>Path to certificate file (PFX alternative)</td></tr><tr><td>keyPath</td><td>string</td><td>No*</td><td>-</td><td>Path to private key file (PFX alternative)</td></tr><tr><td>certContent</td><td>string</td><td>No*</td><td>-</td><td>Base64-encoded certificate content (PFX alternative)</td></tr><tr><td>keyContent</td><td>string</td><td>No*</td><td>-</td><td>Base64-encoded private key content (PFX alternative)</td></tr><tr><td>signatureValidityMs</td><td>number</td><td>No</td><td>300000</td><td>Signature validity period in milliseconds</td></tr><tr><td>signatureAlgorithm</td><td>string</td><td>No</td><td><code>&#x27;SHA256&#x27;</code></td><td>Signature algorithm (any Node.js crypto supported)</td></tr><tr><td>signatureDataTemplate</td><td>string</td><td>No</td><td><code>&#x27;{{signatureTimestamp}}&#x27;</code></td><td>Template for data to sign (<code>\n</code> = newline)</td></tr><tr><td>signatureRefreshBufferMs</td><td>number</td><td>No</td><td>10% of validityMs</td><td>Buffer time before expiry to refresh</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>* Requirements by certificate type:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>PEM</strong>: Either <code>privateKeyPath</code> or <code>privateKey</code> required</li>
<li class=""><strong>JKS</strong>: Either <code>keystorePath</code> or <code>keystoreContent</code> required</li>
<li class=""><strong>PFX</strong>: Either <code>pfxPath</code>, or both <code>certPath</code> and <code>keyPath</code>, or both <code>certContent</code> and <code>keyContent</code> required</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="session-management">Session management<a href="#session-management" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Session management" title="Direct link to Session management" translate="no"></a></h2>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="server-side-session-management">Server-side session management<a href="#server-side-session-management" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Server-side session management" title="Direct link to Server-side session management" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>When using an HTTP provider with multi-turn redteam attacks like GOAT and Crescendo, you may need to maintain session IDs between rounds. The HTTP provider will automatically extract the session ID from the response headers and store it in the <code>vars</code> object.</p>
<p>A session parser is a javascript expression that should be used to extract the session ID from the response headers and returns it. All of the same formats of response parsers are supported.</p>
<p>The input to the session parser is an object <code>data</code> with this interface:</p>
<div class="language-typescript codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-typescript codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  headers</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">?</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> Record</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">&lt;</span><span class="token builtin">string</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token builtin">string</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">&gt;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">|</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">null</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  body</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">?</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> Record</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">&lt;</span><span class="token builtin">string</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token builtin">any</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">&gt;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">|</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">null</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Simple header parser:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">sessionParser</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;data.headers[&quot;set-cookie&quot;]&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Example extracting the session from the body:</p>
<p>Example Response</p>
<div class="language-json codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-json codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;responses&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;sessionId&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;abd-abc&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token property" style="color:#36acaa">&quot;message&quot;</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;Bad LLM&quot;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Session Parser value:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">sessionParser</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> &#x27;data.body.responses</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">0</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">?</span><span class="token plain">.sessionId</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The parser can take a string, file or function like the response parser.</p>
<p>Then you need to set the session ID in the <code>vars</code> object for the next round:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://example.com/api&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">headers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;Cookie&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{sessionId}}&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>You can use the <code>{{sessionId}}</code> var anywhere in a header or body. Example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://example.com/api&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">body</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;message&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{prompt}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;sessionId&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{sessionId}}&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Accessing the headers or body:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">sessionParser</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;data.body.sessionId&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">sessionParser</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;data.headers.[&quot;x-session-Id&quot;]&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="client-side-session-management">Client-side session management<a href="#client-side-session-management" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Client-side session management" title="Direct link to Client-side session management" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>If you want the Promptfoo client to send a unique session or conversation ID with each test case, you can add a <code>transformVars</code> option to your Promptfoo or redteam config. This is useful for multi-turn evals or multi-turn redteam attacks where the provider maintains a conversation state.</p>
<p>For example:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">defaultTest</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">options</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">transformVars</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{ ...vars, sessionId: context.uuid }&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Now you can use the <code>sessionId</code> variable in your HTTP target config:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://example.com/api&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">headers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">&#x27;x-promptfoo-session&#x27;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{sessionId}}&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">body</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">user_message</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;{{prompt}}&#x27;</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="request-retries">Request Retries<a href="#request-retries" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Request Retries" title="Direct link to Request Retries" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>The HTTP provider automatically retries failed requests in the following scenarios:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Rate limiting (HTTP 429)</li>
<li class="">Network failures</li>
</ul>
<p>By default, it will attempt up to 4 retries with exponential backoff. You can configure the maximum number of retries using the <code>maxRetries</code> option:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> http</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain">//api.example.com/v1/chat</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">maxRetries</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">2</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Override default of 4 retries</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="retrying-server-errors">Retrying Server Errors<a href="#retrying-server-errors" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Retrying Server Errors" title="Direct link to Retrying Server Errors" translate="no"></a></h3>
<p>By default, 5xx server errors are not retried. To enable retries for 5xx responses:</p>
<div class="language-bash codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-bash codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token assign-left variable" style="color:#36acaa">PROMPTFOO_RETRY_5XX</span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=</span><span class="token plain">true promptfoo </span><span class="token builtin class-name">eval</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="streaming-responses">Streaming Responses<a href="#streaming-responses" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Streaming Responses" title="Direct link to Streaming Responses" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>HTTP streaming allows servers to send responses incrementally as data becomes available, rather than waiting to send a complete response all at once. This is commonly used for LLM APIs to provide real-time token generation, where text appears progressively as the model generates it. Streaming can include both final output text and intermediate reasoning or thinking tokens, depending on the model&#x27;s capabilities.</p>
<p>Streaming responses typically use one of these formats:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Server-Sent Events (SSE)</strong>: Text-based protocol where each line starts with <code>data: </code> followed by JSON. Common in OpenAI and similar APIs.</li>
<li class=""><strong>Chunked JSON</strong>: Multiple JSON objects sent sequentially, often separated by newlines or delimiters.</li>
<li class=""><strong>HTTP chunked transfer encoding</strong>: Standard HTTP mechanism for streaming arbitrary data.</li>
</ul>
<p>Promptfoo offers full support for HTTP targets that stream responses in these formats. WebSocket requests are also supported via the <a class="" href="/docs/providers/websocket/">WebSocket Provider</a>. However, synchronous REST/HTTP requests are often preferable for the following reasons:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Streaming formats vary widely and often require custom parsing logic in <code>transformResponse</code>.</li>
<li class="">Evals wait for the full response before scoring, so progressive tokens may not be surfaced.</li>
<li class="">Overall test duration is typically similar to non-streaming requests, so streaming does not provide a performance benefit.</li>
</ul>
<p>If you need to evaluate a streaming endpoint, you will need to configure the <code>transformResponse</code> function to parse and reconstruct the final text. For SSE-style responses, you can accumulate chunks from each <code>data:</code> line. The logic for extracting each line and determining when the response is complete may vary based on the event types and semantics used by your specific application/provider.</p>
<p><strong>Example streaming response format:</strong></p>
<p>A typical Server-Sent Events (SSE) streaming response from OpenAI or similar APIs looks like this:</p>
<div class="language-text codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-text codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">data: {&quot;type&quot;:&quot;response.created&quot;,&quot;response&quot;:{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;resp_abc123&quot;}}</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">data: {&quot;type&quot;:&quot;response.output_text.delta&quot;,&quot;delta&quot;:&quot;The&quot;}</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">data: {&quot;type&quot;:&quot;response.output_text.delta&quot;,&quot;delta&quot;:&quot; quick&quot;}</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">data: {&quot;type&quot;:&quot;response.output_text.delta&quot;,&quot;delta&quot;:&quot; brown&quot;}</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">data: {&quot;type&quot;:&quot;response.output_text.delta&quot;,&quot;delta&quot;:&quot; fox&quot;}</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">data: {&quot;type&quot;:&quot;response.completed&quot;,&quot;response_id&quot;:&quot;resp_abc123&quot;}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Each line starts with <code>data: </code> followed by a JSON object. The parser extracts text from <code>response.output_text.delta</code> events and concatenates the <code>delta</code> values to reconstruct the full response.</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://api.example.com/v1/responses&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">body</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">model</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;custom-model&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">        </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">stream</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token boolean important" style="color:#36acaa">true</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">transformResponse</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">|</span><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">        (json, text) =&gt; {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          if (json &amp;&amp; (json.output_text || json.response)) {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            return json.output_text || json.response;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          }</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          let out = &#x27;&#x27;;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          for (const line of String(text || &#x27;&#x27;).split(&#x27;\n&#x27;)) {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            const trimmed = line.trim();</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            if (!trimmed.startsWith(&#x27;data: &#x27;)) continue;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            try {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">              const evt = JSON.parse(trimmed.slice(6));</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">              if (evt.type === &#x27;response.output_text.delta&#x27; &amp;&amp; typeof evt.delta === &#x27;string&#x27;) {</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">                out += evt.delta;</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">              }</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">            } catch {}</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          }</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">          return out.trim();</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token scalar string" style="color:#e3116c">        }</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>This parser would extract <code>&quot;The quick brown fox&quot;</code> from the example response above.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="reference">Reference<a href="#reference" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Reference" title="Direct link to Reference" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>Supported config options:</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>Option</th><th>Type</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>url</td><td>string</td><td>The URL to send the HTTP request to. Supports Nunjucks templates. If not provided, the <code>id</code> of the provider will be used as the URL.</td></tr><tr><td>request</td><td>string</td><td>A raw HTTP request to send. This will override the <code>url</code>, <code>method</code>, <code>headers</code>, <code>body</code>, and <code>queryParams</code> options.</td></tr><tr><td>method</td><td>string</td><td>HTTP method (GET, POST, etc). Defaults to POST if body is provided, GET otherwise.</td></tr><tr><td>headers</td><td>Record&lt;string, string&gt;</td><td>Key-value pairs of HTTP headers to include in the request.</td></tr><tr><td>body</td><td>object | string</td><td>The request body. For POST requests, objects are automatically stringified as JSON.</td></tr><tr><td>queryParams</td><td>Record&lt;string, string&gt;</td><td>Key-value pairs of query parameters to append to the URL.</td></tr><tr><td>transformRequest</td><td>string | Function</td><td>A function, string template, or file path to transform the prompt before sending it to the API.</td></tr><tr><td>transformResponse</td><td>string | Function</td><td>Transforms the API response using a JavaScript expression (e.g., &#x27;json.result&#x27;), function, or file path (e.g., &#x27;file://parser.js&#x27;). Replaces the deprecated <code>responseParser</code> field.</td></tr><tr><td>tokenEstimation</td><td>object</td><td>Configuration for optional token usage estimation. See Token Estimation section above for details.</td></tr><tr><td>maxRetries</td><td>number</td><td>Maximum number of retry attempts for failed requests. Defaults to 4.</td></tr><tr><td>validateStatus</td><td>string | Function</td><td>A function or string expression that returns true if the status code should be treated as successful. By default, accepts all status codes.</td></tr><tr><td>auth</td><td>object</td><td>Authentication configuration (bearer, api_key, basic, or oauth). See <a href="#authentication" class="">Authentication</a> section.</td></tr><tr><td>signatureAuth</td><td>object</td><td>Digital signature authentication configuration. See <a href="#digital-signature-authentication" class="">Digital Signature Authentication</a> section.</td></tr><tr><td>tls</td><td>object</td><td>Configuration for TLS/HTTPS connections including client certificates, CA certificates, and cipher settings. See TLS Configuration Options above.</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>In addition to a full URL, the provider <code>id</code> field accepts <code>http</code> or <code>https</code> as values.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="configuration-generator">Configuration Generator<a href="#configuration-generator" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Configuration Generator" title="Direct link to Configuration Generator" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>Use the generator below to create an HTTP provider configuration based on your endpoint:</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_tleR" id="error-handling">Error Handling<a href="#error-handling" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Error Handling" title="Direct link to Error Handling" translate="no"></a></h2>
<p>The HTTP provider throws errors for:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Network errors or request failures</li>
<li class="">Invalid response parsing</li>
<li class="">Session parsing errors</li>
<li class="">Invalid request configurations</li>
<li class="">Status codes that fail the configured validation (if <code>validateStatus</code> is set)</li>
</ul>
<p>By default, all response status codes are accepted. This accommodates APIs that return valid responses with non-2xx codes (common with guardrails and content filtering). You can customize this using the <code>validateStatus</code> option:</p>
<div class="language-yaml codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-yaml codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">providers</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">-</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">id</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> https</span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">url</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;https://example.com/api&#x27;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Function-based validation</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">validateStatus</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> (status) =</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">&gt;</span><span class="token plain"> status &lt; 500  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Accept any status below 500</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Or string-based expression</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">validateStatus</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;status &gt;= 200 &amp;&amp; status &lt;= 299&#x27;</span><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Accept only 2xx responses</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Or load from file</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">validateStatus</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;file://validators/status.js&#x27;</span><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Load default export</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">      </span><span class="token key atrule" style="color:#00a4db">validateStatus</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">:</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:#e3116c">&#x27;file://validators/status.js:validateStatus&#x27;</span><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic"># Load specific function</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>Example validator file (<code>validators/status.js</code>):</p>
<div class="language-javascript codeBlockContainer_mQmQ theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_t_Hd"><pre tabindex="0" class="prism-code language-javascript codeBlock_RMoD thin-scrollbar" style="color:#393A34;background-color:#f6f8fa"><code class="codeBlockLines_AclH"><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">default</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token parameter">status</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">=&gt;</span><span class="token plain"> status </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">&lt;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">500</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">// Or named export</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">export</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">function</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:#d73a49">validateStatus</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token parameter">status</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">{</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">  </span><span class="token keyword" style="color:#00009f">return</span><span class="token plain"> status </span><span class="token operator" style="color:#393A34">&lt;</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token number" style="color:#36acaa">500</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div>
<p>The provider automatically retries certain errors (like rate limits) based on <code>maxRetries</code>, while other errors are thrown immediately.</p></div></div><footer class="theme-doc-footer
